@resolution_weight_hated = 3
@resolution_weight_disliked = 4
@resolution_weight_unpopular = 5
@resolution_weight_normal = 6
@resolution_weight_popular = 6.5
@resolution_weight_loved = 7
@resolution_weight_fever = 10

@resolution_cost_t1 = 100
@resolution_cost_t2 = 150
@resolution_cost_t3 = 200
@resolution_cost_t4 = 250
@resolution_cost_t5 = 300
@resolution_cost_denounce = 25

@resolution_cost_t1_half = 50
@resolution_cost_t2_half = 75
@resolution_cost_t3_half = 100
@resolution_cost_t4_half = 125
@resolution_cost_t5_half = 150
@resolution_cost_denounce_half = 12.5

@resolution_flag_timer = 360

# <5.5	反对
# >7	赞成
# <1	一票否决
# >10	紧急措施
# 下一个比这一个好+3	冻结
# 比反对低2 / 比赞成高2	申请外交支援

resolution_declare_crisis_empire = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_declare_crisis"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			trigger = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" } }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5_half
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = yes

	valid_target = {
		NOT = { is_same_value = from }
		is_galactic_emperor = no
		OR = {
			is_country_type = default
			AND = {
				is_fallen_empire = yes
				NOT = { has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing }
			}
			OR = { #兼容Expanded Diplomacy and Espionage
				is_country_type = ascended_empire
				is_country_type = lost_empire
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_the_step_towards_a_united_galaxy }
			is_galactic_community_member = no
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = declared_crisis }
	}

	modifier = {
		starbase_shipyard_build_speed_mult = 0.20
		ships_upkeep_mult = -0.1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_declare_crisis_empire_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				remove_from_galactic_community = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_council_established = yes
					is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				}
				remove_from_galactic_council = yes
			}
			every_subject = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
					remove_from_galactic_community = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_galactic_council_established = yes
						is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
					}
					remove_from_galactic_council = yes
				}
			}

			set_country_flag = declared_crisis
			save_event_target_as = new_crisis
			country_event = { id = crisis.4106 }
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
					NOT = { is_same_value = prev }
				}
				country_event = { id = crisis.4101 }
			}
			galactic_emperor = {
				save_event_target_as = community_war_leader
			}
			declare_crisis_war_effect = yes
			if = { #兼容 Expanded Diplomacy and Espionage
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = better_diplo_installed
					from = { has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis }
					NOR = {
						is_homicidal = yes
						has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
						AND = {
							is_fallen_empire = yes
							NOT = { has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing }
						}
					}
				}
				from = { complete_crisis_objective = crisobj_perform_upsetting_operations }
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_hated

		# Should almost always declare on Crisis countries in end game
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			from = {
				has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}

		# More likely to declare on very powerful homicidal empires
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			from = {
				is_homicidal = yes
				relative_power = {
					who = prev
					category = fleet
					value = overwhelming
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_target_is_very_strong_homicidal_empire
		}
		# More likely to declare on very powerful homicidal empires
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			from = {
				is_homicidal = yes
				relative_power = {
					who = prev
					category = fleet
					value = superior
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_target_is_strong_homicidal_empire
		}

		# More likely to declare on rivals
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_rival = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}

		# Never on yourself
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_same_value = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_me
		}

		# More likely to declare on empire who hvae cracked a star
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			from = { has_country_flag = cracked_first_star }
			desc = gal_com_target_has_cracked_stars
		}

		# Should be reluctant to use on normal countries
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			OR = {
				from = {
					is_homicidal = no
					NOR = {
						has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed
						has_country_flag = cracked_first_star
					}
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_target_is_a_normal_empire
		}

		# Very unlikely to use on Custodian
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			from = { is_galactic_custodian = yes }
			desc = gal_com_target_is_the_custodian
		}

		# Unlikely to use on scary Fallen Empire
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			from = {
				is_fallen_empire = yes
				relative_power = {
					who = prev
					category = fleet
					value = overwhelming
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_target_is_powerful_fallen_empire
		}
	}
}

resolution_custodian_galactic_standard = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_standard"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_galactic_standard } }
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_galactic_standard = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_galactic_standard }
			has_global_flag = flag_galactic_standard_set_timer
		}
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_galactic_standard_price = 1 }
	}

	effect = {
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_isolationist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_supremacist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_standard_set } }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_standard_price_effect"
				set_global_flag = flag_galactic_standard_set
				set_timed_global_flag = {
					flag = flag_galactic_standard_set_timer
					years = 25
				}
				event_target:global_event_country = {
					set_saved_date = {
						key = galactic_standard_set_timer
						days_from_present = 9000
						expires = 9000
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = galactic_standard_activated
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_standard_set_timer }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_standard_price_effect_active"
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_standard }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_republic_formed } # for compatibility with Expanded Diplomacy and Espionage mod 
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_custodian = yes
		#NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_galactic_standard }
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = peaceful_traders
				has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists
			}
			desc = gal_com_trader_ai_personality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}
}
resolution_custodian_science_cooperation_initiative = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_custodian_science_cooperation_initiative"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_custodian_science_cooperation_initiative = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_science_cooperation_initiative_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
				}
				every_owned_leader = {
					limit = {
						leader_class = scientist
						OR = {
							is_researching_area = physics
							is_researching_area = society
							is_researching_area = engineering
						}
					}
					add_skill = 1
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = flag_resolution_custodian_science_cooperation_initiative
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_science_cooperation_initiative" }
		}
		has_technology = tech_global_research_initiative
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_galactic_standard_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_galactic_standard_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_galactic_standard"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_galactic_standard"
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_galacticstudies_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_galacticstudies_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_cooperative_research_channels"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_extradimensional_experimentation"
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_custodian = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_fever

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_spiritualist = yes
			desc = ethic_spiritualist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5

resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries_custodian = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value = pathetic }
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries_pathetic = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value = inferior }
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries_inferior = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value = equivalent }
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries_equivalent = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value >= superior }
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries_superior = 1
		}
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_galactic_custodian = yes }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries_effect_custodian"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value <= inferior } }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries_effect_weaker"
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries_effect_stronger"
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_gto"
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_custodian = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value = pathetic }
			desc = gal_com_relative_economy_power_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value = inferior }
			desc = gal_com_relative_economy_power_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value >= equivalent }
			desc = gal_com_relative_economy_power_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			relative_power = { who = galactic_custodian category = economy value >= superior }
			desc = gal_com_relative_economy_power_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
	}

resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_megacorp = no
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness }
			any_country = {
				is_criminal_syndicate = yes
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_anti_inner = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			any_owned_planet = {
				has_branch_office = yes
				branch_office_owner = {
					is_criminal_syndicate = yes
					is_galactic_community_member = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_anti_outer = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_criminal_syndicate = yes
		}
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_criminal = 1 }
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galpol
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_effect"
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_megacorp = no
				NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_criminal_syndicate = yes
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_effect_anti_inner"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_criminal_syndicate = yes
						is_galactic_community_member = no
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_effect_anti_outer"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_criminal_syndicate = no
				is_megacorp = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_effect_megacorp"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_effect_gestalt"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_criminal_syndicate = yes
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_crack_down_on_criminal_syndicate_effect_criminal"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_criminal_syndicate = yes
				is_galactic_community_member = no
			}

resolution_custodian_peace_windows_project = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_custodian_peace_windows_project"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_custodian_peace_windows_project = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_peace_windows_project_tooltip"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = peace_windows_project
			every_war = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						using_war_goal = {
							type = wg_declared_crisis
							owner = attacker
						}
					}
					any_attacker = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
					any_defender = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				}
				every_war_participant = {
					limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
					prev = { remove_war_participant = prev }
					country_event = { id = emperor.360 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_peace_windows_project" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_perpetual_custodianship
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life_or_higher_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life_or_higher_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life
				is_active_resolution = resolution_rulesofwar_independent_tribunals
				is_active_resolution = resolution_rulesofwar_last_resort_doctrine
				is_active_resolution = resolution_rulesofwar_demobilization_initiative
				is_active_resolution = resolution_rulesofwar_6
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
		NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_pax_galactica }
	}

	active = {
		OR = {
			has_galactic_custodian = yes
			has_galactic_emperor = yes
		}
		NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_pax_galactica }
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_gestalt = yes
			desc = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
	}

		potential = { eci_mod_activated = yes is_gal_confed_member = yes federation = { has_federation_law = centralization_very_high_confederation } has_global_flag = confederation_purpose_eci_capitalism }
		modifier = { confederation_purpose_eci_capitalism = 5 }
	}
	#################################### 邦联基石
	# 普通和霸权联邦的基石效果直接在法案里
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_gestalt = no
			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = confederation_bedrock_trade }
		}
		modifier = { confederation_bedrock_trade = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_gestalt = yes
			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = confederation_bedrock_trade }
		}
		modifier = { confederation_bedrock_trade_gestalt = 1 }
	}

			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = confederation_bedrock_research }
		}
		modifier = { confederation_bedrock_research = 1 }

			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = confederation_bedrock_spiritualist }
		}
		modifier = { confederation_bedrock_spiritualist = 1 }
	}
	#################################### 集权度
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = centralization_minimal_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { law_category_centralization_confederation = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = centralization_low_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { law_category_centralization_confederation = 2 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = centralization_medium_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { law_category_centralization_confederation = 3 }
	}

		potential = {
			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = centralization_high_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { law_category_centralization_confederation = 4 }
	}

			has_federation = yes
			federation = { has_federation_law = centralization_very_high_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { law_category_centralization_confederation = 5 }
	}

	triggered_modifier = {

			has_federation = yes

	triggered_modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {
			treaties_separate_no_confederation_modifier = 1
		}
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				galactic_custodian = {
					has_federation = yes
					federation = { NOT = { has_federation_flag = special_federation } }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_establish_the_galactic_confederation_effect_custodian_federation"
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_establish_the_galactic_confederation_effect"
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			galactic_custodian = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_establish_the_galactic_confederation } }
					country_event = {
						id = MECR.2000
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_timed_global_flag = {
				flag = resolution_custodian_establish_the_galactic_confederation
				days = 360
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_establish_the_galactic_confederation" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_perpetual_custodianship
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_peace_windows_project
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_standard
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_gdf
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galpol
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "no_partners_in_community"
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				is_galactic_custodian = no
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { #兼容帝皇起源 #已取消限制
			fail_text = "domination_of_custodian_is_not_firm_yet__galactic_confederation_pre_timer"
			always = yes
			#if = {

			#		mid_game_years_passed >= 0
			#		has_global_flag = flag_debug_skip_geo_time_limit
			#	}
			#}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_republic_formed }
	}

	active = {
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_establish_the_galactic_confederation
			any_federation = { has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_egalitarian = yes
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = peaceful_traders
				has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists
			}
			desc = gal_com_trader_ai_personality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ai_personality = federation_builders
			desc = gal_com_federation_builders_ai_personality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			is_authoritarian = no
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness }
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			OR = {
				is_authoritarian = yes
				has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
			}
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			is_authoritarian = no
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}

			gdf_naval_cap_2 = 1
		}
	}
	################################# 银河邦联提供的额外舰容
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = independent_gdf
			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
			any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_low_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { country_naval_cap_add = 40 }
	}

			any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_medium_confederation }

			any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_combined_fleet_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { country_naval_cap_add = 200 }
	}
	
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = gdf_expand_size value = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_gdf"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			any_playable_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_declared_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {

resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_3 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_expand_gdf"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_3" }
		}
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_custodian_gdf_3 = 1
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			NOT = {
				any_federation = {
					has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive
					OR = {
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_low_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_medium_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_high_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_very_high_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_combined_fleet_confederation
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = { country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 400 }
	}
	################################# 银河邦联提供的额外舰容
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_low_confederation } }

	}

	}

	triggered_modifier = {

			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
		}
		modifier = {
			gdf_naval_cap_3 = 1
		}

		modifier = { country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 600 }
	}
	
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = independent_gdf
			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
		}
		modifier = {
			gdf_naval_cap_5 = 1
		}
	}
	################################# 银河邦联提供的额外舰容
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = independent_gdf
			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
			any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_low_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { country_naval_cap_add = 40 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = independent_gdf
			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
			any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_medium_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { country_naval_cap_add = 80 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = independent_gdf
			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
			any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_high_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { country_naval_cap_add = 120 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = independent_gdf
			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
			any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_very_high_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { country_naval_cap_add = 160 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = independent_gdf
			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
			any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_combined_fleet_confederation }
		}
		modifier = { country_naval_cap_add = 200 }
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = gdf_expand_size value = 5 }
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_4"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			any_playable_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_declared_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
			desc = gal_com_we_have_crisis_perk
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			is_militarist = yes
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_militarist_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_subject_of_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			desc = gal_com_exists_awakened_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_ongoing_war_in_heaven
		}
	}
}
resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_6 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_expand_gdf"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_6" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_establish_the_galactic_confederation
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_custodian_gdf_6 = 1
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			NOT = {
				any_federation = {
					has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive
					OR = {
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_low_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_medium_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_high_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_very_high_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_combined_fleet_confederation
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = { country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 400 }
	}
	################################# 银河邦联提供的额外舰容
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_low_confederation } }
		modifier = { country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 440 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_medium_confederation } }
		modifier = { country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 480 }

		potential = { any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_very_high_confederation } }

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { any_federation = { has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_combined_fleet_confederation } }
		modifier = { country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 600 }
	}
	
	triggered_modifier = {

			has_global_flag = independent_gdf
			is_same_value = event_target:gdf_country
		}

		}
		modifier = {

		}

	################################# 银河邦联提供的额外舰容
	triggered_modifier = {

		}
		modifier = { country_naval_cap_add = 200 }
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = gdf_expand_size value = 8 }
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_7"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			any_playable_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_declared_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
			desc = gal_com_we_have_crisis_perk
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			is_militarist = yes
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_militarist_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_subject_of_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			desc = gal_com_exists_awakened_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_ongoing_war_in_heaven
		}
	}

		}

		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"

	}

		resolution_custodian_gdf_9 = 1

			NOT = {
				any_federation = {
					has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive
					OR = {
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_low_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_medium_confederation
						has_federation_law = fleet_contribution_high_confederation

resolution_custodian_reduce_gdf = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_reduce_gdf"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_reduce_gdf_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_10" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_10"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_9" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_9"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_8" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_8"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_7" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_7"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_6" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_6"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_5" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_5"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_4" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_4"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_3" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_3"
			}
			else = {
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf"
			}
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				subtract_variable = { which = gdf_expand_size value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		has_galactic_emperor = no
		OR = {
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
		}
		OR = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_3"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_4"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_5"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_6"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_7"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_8"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_9"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_expand_gdf_10"
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_playable_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
			desc = gal_com_we_have_crisis_perk
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_subject_of_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			desc = gal_com_exists_awakened_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_ongoing_war_in_heaven
		}
	}
}

					is_galactic_emperor = no

						who = PREV
						level >= good
					}
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_reliable_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}

resolution_emperor_take_over_power_of_council = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_take_over_power_of_council"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_emperor = no
					is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					who = galactic_emperor
					modifier = opinion_resolution_emperor_take_over_power_of_council
				}
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_emperor = yes
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
		num_council_positions > 0
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			galactic_emperor = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			any_country = {
				is_ai = no
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				galactic_emperor = {
					opinion_level = {
						who = PREV
						level <= poor
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					is_ai = no
					is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
					galactic_emperor = {
						opinion_level = {
							who = PREV
							level >= good
						}
					}
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_unreliable_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}
}

resolution_emperor_by_appointment = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_imperial_council_appointment"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_by_appointment_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
					is_galactic_emperor = no
				}
				add_permanent_councillor = yes
			}
			set_emperor_can_change_council_members = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_trial_of_advancement" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_trial_of_advancement"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_by_election" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_by_election"
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_by_appointment" }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_hated

		cost = {

		}

		}

		}

		}

			factor = 6
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8

			desc = gal_com_someone_declared_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
			desc = gal_com_we_have_crisis_perk
		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			is_militarist = yes

			desc = militarist_galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {

		}
	}

resolution_emperor_clean_up_ancient_threats = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_clean_up_ancient_threats"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			trigger = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" } }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4_half
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		description = resolution_emperor_clean_up_ancient_threats_modifier_desc
		damage_vs_country_type_fallen_empire_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_awakened_fallen_empire_mult = 0.25
	
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_dragon_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_stellarite_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_wraith_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_hiver_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_horror_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_fortress_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_dreadnought_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_sphere_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_scavenger_bot_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_elderly_tiyanki_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_guardian_hatchling_mult = 0.25
	
		damage_vs_country_type_gate_builders_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_gray_goo_mult = 0.25
		damage_vs_country_type_ldragon_country_mult = 0.25
	
		country_unity_produces_mult = -0.05
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_clean_up_ancient_threats }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_have_an_ancient_threat"
			OR = {
				any_country = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
				any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
				any_country = { is_country_type = gate_builders }
				has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
				any_country = {
					is_guardian_country = yes
					count_owned_fleet = { count > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
			AND = {
				is_galactic_custodian = yes
				has_global_flag = galactic_republic_formed	#Expanded Diplomacy and Espionage mod
			}
		}
	}

	active = {
		OR = {
			has_galactic_emperor = yes
			has_global_flag = galactic_republic_formed		#Expanded Diplomacy and Espionage mod
		}
		OR = {
			any_country = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			any_country = { is_country_type = gate_builders }
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			any_country = {
				is_guardian_country = yes
				count_owned_fleet = { count > 0 }
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_hated

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.6
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOR = {
				has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
				has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_xenophile = yes
			NOR = {
				has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
				has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_subject_of_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_neighbor_country = {
				is_country_type = gray_goo
			}
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_gray_goo
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_militarist = yes
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = militarist_galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			desc = gal_com_exists_awakened_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_country = {
				is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
				is_at_war_with = prev
			}
			desc = gal_com_having_awr_with_awakened_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_ongoing_war_in_heaven
		}
	}
}

resolution_emperor_standardizing_weights_and_measures = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_standardizing_weights_and_measures"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_emperor_standardizing_weights_and_measures = 1
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = flag_standardizing_weights_and_measures_set_timer
		}
		modifier = { resolution_emperor_standardizing_weights_and_measures_price = 1 }
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = flag_standardizing_weights_and_measures_set } }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_emperor_standardizing_weights_and_measures_price_effect"
				set_global_flag = flag_standardizing_weights_and_measures_set
				set_timed_global_flag = {
					flag = flag_standardizing_weights_and_measures_set_timer
					years = 10
				}
				event_target:global_event_country = {
					set_saved_date = {
						key = standardizing_weights_and_measures_set_timer
						days_from_present = 3600
						expires = 3600
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = flag_standardizing_weights_and_measures_set_timer }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_emperor_standardizing_weights_and_measures_price_effect_active"
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_standardizing_weights_and_measures" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_galactic_standard"
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}

resolution_emperor_reduce_government_agencies = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_reduce_government_agencies"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_expand_government_agencies }
		}
		modifier = {
			building_imperial_government_cap = -1
			country_unity_produces_mult = 0.08
		}
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_expand_government_agencies }
			tooltip = { cancel_resolution = resolution_emperor_expand_government_agencies }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_galactic_emperor = no }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_emperor_reduce_government_agencies_effect"
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_reduce_government_agencies" }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_keep_at_least_one_building_imperial_government"
			check_variable_arithmetic = { which = galactic_emperor.modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value > 0 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "building_imperial_government_has_reached_cap"
			NOR = {
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count > 0 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = galactic_emperor.modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 0 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count > 1 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = galactic_emperor.modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 1 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count > 2 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = galactic_emperor.modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 2 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count > 3 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = galactic_emperor.modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 3 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count > 4 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = galactic_emperor.modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 4 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count > 5 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = galactic_emperor.modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		has_technology = tech_galactic_administration
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count < 1 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 1 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count < 2 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 2 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count < 3 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 3 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count < 4 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 4 }
				}
				AND = {
					count_owned_planet = { limit = { has_building = building_imperial_government } count < 5 }
					check_variable_arithmetic = { which = modifier:building_imperial_government_cap value = 5 }
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_dont_need_so_many_building_imperial_government
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_egalitarian = yes
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			opinion_level = {
				who = galactic_emperor
				level <= poor
			}
			desc = gal_com_opinion_to_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			opinion_level = {
				who = galactic_emperor
				level >= good
			}
			desc = gal_com_opinion_to_emperor
		}
	}
}

resolution_emperor_the_step_towards_a_united_galaxy = { # 整合星海帝国——所有成员国拉进帝国联邦
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_the_step_towards_a_united_galaxy"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = 500
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_the_step_towards_a_united_galaxy_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			galactic_emperor = {
				country_event = {
					id = MECR.1000
				}
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		imperial_authority = 200
		is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_pax_galactica
		is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_armada
		is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_galactic_standard
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "no_partners_in_empire"
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				is_galactic_emperor = no
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_the_step_towards_a_united_galaxy" }
		}
		custom_tooltip = { #兼容帝皇起源
			fail_text = "domination_of_imperium_is_not_firm_yet__the_step_towards_a_united_galaxy_pre_timer"
			if = {
				limit = { has_origin = origin_galactic_hegemon }
				OR = {
					years_passed >= 75
					mid_game_years_passed >= 0
					has_global_flag = flag_debug_skip_geo_time_limit
				}
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
		any_federation = { has_federation_perk = imperium_federation_passive }
	}

	breach = {
		has_federation = yes
		federation = { has_federation_perk = imperium_federation_passive }
		is_gestalt = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				federation = { has_federation_law = imperium_ai_policy_ai_outlawed }
				OR = {
					has_policy_flag = ai_servitude
					has_policy_flag = ai_full_rights
				}
			}
			AND = {
				federation = { has_federation_law = imperium_ai_policy_ai_servitude }
				OR = {
					has_policy_flag = ai_outlawed
					has_policy_flag = ai_full_rights
				}
			}
			AND = {
				federation = { has_federation_law = imperium_ai_policy_ai_full_rights }
				OR = {
					has_policy_flag = ai_outlawed
					has_policy_flag = ai_servitude
				}
			}

			AND = {
				federation = { has_federation_law = imperium_slavery_policy_slavery_not_allowed }
				has_policy_flag = slavery_allowed
			}
			AND = {
				federation = { has_federation_law = imperium_slavery_policy_slavery_allowed }
				has_policy_flag = slavery_not_allowed
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = peaceful_traders
				has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists
			}
			desc = gal_com_trader_ai_personality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ai_personality = federation_builders
			desc = gal_com_federation_builders_ai_personality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }

resolution_emperor_imperial_unification = { # 整合星海帝国——吞并所有政体兼容的国家，游戏胜利
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_imperial_unification"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = { influence = 750 }
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
		modifier = { country_government_civic_points_add = 1 }
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_unification_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				country_event = {
					id = MECR.1102
				}
			}
			galactic_emperor = {
				# 调整议会法案，移除常任
				if = {
					limit = { is_galactic_council_established = no }
					cancel_resolution = resolution_emperor_abolish_council
					pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_emperor_restore_council
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_by_appointment } }
					cancel_resolution = resolution_emperor_trial_of_advancement
					cancel_resolution = resolution_emperor_by_election
					pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_emperor_by_appointment
				}
				cancel_resolution = resolution_emperor_permanent_seat
				cancel_resolution = resolution_emperor_revoke_permanent_seat
				# 开始吞并
				country_event = {
					id = MECR.1100
				}
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		every_federation = {
			limit = { has_federation_perk = imperium_federation_passive }
			add_cohesion = -150
		}
		add_imperial_authority = -100
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_unification" }
		}
		imperial_authority = 200
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_unification" } }
			galactic_emperor.federation = {
				has_federation_perk = imperium_unify
				has_federation_law = centralization_imperium_max
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { #兼容帝皇起源
			fail_text = "domination_of_imperium_is_not_firm_yet__imperial_unification_pre_timer"
			if = {
				limit = { has_origin = origin_galactic_hegemon }
				OR = {
					years_passed >= 150
					end_game_years_passed >= 0
					has_global_flag = flag_debug_skip_geo_time_limit
				}
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_emperor = yes
		any_federation = {
			has_federation_perk = imperium_federation_passive
		}
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
		any_federation = { has_federation_perk = imperium_federation_passive }
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			desc = gal_com_emperors_subject
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ai_personality = federation_builders
			desc = gal_com_federation_builders_ai_personality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			opinion_level = {
				who = galactic_emperor
				level = excellent
			}
			desc = gal_com_opinion_to_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			opinion_level = {
				who = galactic_emperor
				level = good
			}
			desc = gal_com_opinion_to_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			opinion_level = {
				who = galactic_emperor
				level = neutral
			}
			desc = gal_com_opinion_to_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			opinion_level = {
				who = galactic_emperor
				level <= poor
			}
			desc = gal_com_opinion_to_emperor
		}
	}
}

################################### resolution_category_emperor_imperial_institutions
resolution_emperor_imperial_bank = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_imperial_bank"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = no
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_emperor_imperial_bank = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_emperor_imperial_bank_emperor = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求
		potential = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 200 }
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "non_repealable_department"
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_federation = no
					federation = {
						NOR = {
							has_federation_law = imperial_bank_administration
							has_federation_law = imperial_bank_control
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_emperor_imperial_bank_effect_emperor"
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_galactic_emperor = no }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_emperor_imperial_bank_effect_other"
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			galactic_emperor = {
				country_event = {
					id = MECR.1991
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_bank" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_galactic_standard"
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_commerce_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_commerce_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_buzzword_standardization"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_leveraged_privateering"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_underdeveloped_system_utilization"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_holistic_asset_coordination"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_profit_maximization_engines"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_6"
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "can_support_less_upgraded_institutions_resolution"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_bank
				NOT = { any_federation = { has_federation_perk = imperium_federation_passive } }
				federation = {
					check_variable = {
						which = imperial_institutions_upgrades_support
						value > value:imperial_institutions_upgrades_used
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = peaceful_traders
				has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists
			}
			desc = gal_com_trader_ai_personality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			desc = gal_com_emperors_subject
		}
	}
}

					}

	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求
		potential = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 250 }
	}
	

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_education_effect_emperor
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_galactic_emperor = no
				galactic_emperor = {
					is_regular_empire = yes
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_education_effect_other_ep_regular
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_galactic_emperor = no
				galactic_emperor = {
					has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_education_effect_other_ep_gestalt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_galactic_emperor = no
				is_regular_empire = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_education_effect_other_regular
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_galactic_emperor = no
				has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
			}
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_education_effect_other_gestalt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#cancel_resolution = resolution_emperor_disband_imperial_ministry_of_education
			galactic_emperor = {
				country_event = {
					id = MECR.1995
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_education" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_galactic_standard"
		imperial_authority >= 140
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "can_support_less_upgraded_institutions_resolution"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_education
				NOT = { any_federation = { has_federation_perk = imperium_federation_passive } }
				federation = {
					check_variable = {
						which = imperial_institutions_upgrades_support
						value > value:imperial_institutions_upgrades_used
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_egalitarian = yes
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			desc = gal_com_emperors_subject
		}
	}
}

		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence"
		if = {
			limit = {
				galactic_emperor = {
					has_federation = yes
					federation = { has_federation_perk = imperium_federation_passive }
				}
			}
			galactic_emperor = {
				federation = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_federation_law = imperial_armada_conscription_low
								has_federation_law = imperial_armada_conscription_mid
								has_federation_law = imperial_armada_conscription_high
							}
						}
						set_federation_law = imperial_armada_conscription_none
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}

resolution_emperor_imperial_armada = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_imperial_armada"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_emperor_ia = 1
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			galactic_emperor = {
				has_federation = yes
				federation = { has_federation_law = imperial_ministry_of_defence_joint_headquarter }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 100
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求
		potential = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage_naval = 200 }
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_armada" }
		}
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { galactic_defense_force_exists = no } #e.g. Custodian becomes Emperor
			set_galactic_defense_force = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = emperor.50 }
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
		NOT = {
			any_country = { has_country_flag = gdf_turned_into_armada }
		}
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			any_playable_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_declared_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			desc = gal_com_emperors_subject
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_subject_of_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			desc = gal_com_exists_awakened_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_ongoing_war_in_heaven
		}
	}
