	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_emperor_ia_2 = 1
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			NOT = {
				galactic_emperor = {
					has_federation = yes
					federation = { has_federation_law = imperial_ministry_of_defence_joint_headquarter }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 400
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			galactic_emperor = {
				has_federation = yes
				federation = { has_federation_law = imperial_ministry_of_defence_joint_headquarter }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 500
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求
		potential = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage_naval = 100 }
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_armada"
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			any_playable_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_declared_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			desc = gal_com_emperors_subject
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			desc = gal_com_exists_awakened_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_ongoing_war_in_heaven
		}
	}

resolution_emperor_expand_ia_7 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_expand_armada"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			trigger = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" } }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1_half
		}
	}
	target = no

	allow = {
		imperial_authority >= 100
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_7" }
		}
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_emperor_ia_7 = 1
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			NOT = {
				galactic_emperor = {
					has_federation = yes
					federation = { has_federation_law = imperial_ministry_of_defence_joint_headquarter }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 400
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			galactic_emperor = {
				has_federation = yes
				federation = { has_federation_law = imperial_ministry_of_defence_joint_headquarter }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			country_community_gdf_naval_capacity = 500
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求
		potential = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage_naval = 100 }
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_6"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {

			influence = @resolution_cost_t1_half
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_emperor_reduce_ia_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_10" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_10"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_9" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_9"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_8" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_8"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_7" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_7"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_6" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_6"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_5" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_5"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_4" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_4"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_3" }
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_3"
			}
			else = {
				cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia"
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
		OR = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_3"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_4"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_5"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_6"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_7"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_8"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_9"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_ia_10"
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_playable_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
			desc = gal_com_we_have_crisis_perk
		}
		modifier = {

			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = fallen_empire
					is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire

			factor = 0.2

		}

resolution_emperor_imperial_legions = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_imperial_legions"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			trigger = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" } }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3_half
		}
	}
	target = no

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_legions" }
		}
	}

	modifier = {
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求
		potential = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage_naval = 125 }
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_legions_tooltip_basic
		if = {
			limit = { galactic_emperor = { NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness } } }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_legions_tooltip_emperor_is_regular
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { galactic_emperor = { is_machine_empire = yes } }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_legions_tooltip_emperor_is_machine
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_legions_tooltip_emperor_is_hive
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_legions
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = resolution_emperor_imperial_legions_tooltip_count
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			galactic_emperor = {
				#招募界面的显示
				set_variable = { which = imperial_legion_soldier_count value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = imperial_legion_soldier_count_mega_warform value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = imperial_legion_soldier_count_warrior_drones value = 0 }
				every_owned_army = {
					limit = {
						is_defensive_army = no
						OR = {
							army_type = imperial_legion
							army_type = imperial_mega_warform
							army_type = imperial_warrior_drones
						}
					}
					switch = {
						trigger = army_type
						imperial_legion = { prev = { change_variable = { which = imperial_legion_soldier_count value = 1 } } }
						imperial_mega_warform = { prev = { change_variable = { which = imperial_legion_soldier_count_mega_warform value = 1 } } }
						imperial_warrior_drones = { prev = { change_variable = { which = imperial_legion_soldier_count_warrior_drones value = 1 } } }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { which = var_imperial_legion_cap value = value:imperial_legion_cap }
				set_variable = { which = var_imperial_mega_warform_cap value = value:imperial_mega_warform_cap }
				set_variable = { which = var_imperial_warrior_drones_cap value = value:imperial_warrior_drones_cap }

				if = { #给ai皇帝招募20支帝国军团，机械优先，普通和蜂群随机
					limit = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
					while = {
						count = 20
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									which = "imperial_legion_soldier_count_mega_warform"
									value < value:imperial_mega_warform_cap
								}
							}
							capital_scope = {
								create_army = {
									owner = galactic_emperor
									type = "imperial_mega_warform"
								}
							}
							change_variable = {
								which = "imperial_legion_soldier_count_mega_warform"
								value = 1
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									check_variable = {
										which = "imperial_legion_soldier_count"
										value < value:imperial_legion_cap
									}
									check_variable = {
										which = "imperial_legion_soldier_count_warrior_drones"
										value < value:imperial_warrior_drones_cap
									}
								}
							}
							random_list = {
								10 = {
									modifier = {
										factor = 0
										NOT = {
											check_variable = {
												which = "imperial_legion_soldier_count"
												value < value:imperial_legion_cap
											}
										}
									}
									capital_scope = {
										create_army = {
											owner = galactic_emperor
											type = "imperial_legion"
										}
									}
									change_variable = {
										which = "imperial_legion_soldier_count"
										value = 1
									}
								}
								10 = {
									modifier = {
										factor = 0
										NOT = {
											check_variable = {
												which = "imperial_legion_soldier_count_warrior_drones"
												value < value:imperial_warrior_drones_cap
											}
										}
									}
									capital_scope = {
										create_army = {
											owner = galactic_emperor
											type = "imperial_warrior_drones"
										}
									}
									change_variable = {
										which = "imperial_legion_soldier_count_warrior_drones"
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = emperor.55 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
	}

	active = {
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_xenophobe = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			any_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			desc = gal_com_neighboring_crisis_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			has_crisis_stage_2 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			any_playable_country = { has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed }
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 14
			any_playable_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
			desc = gal_com_someone_declared_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = gray_goo_crisis_active
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 14
			has_global_flag = marauder_crisis_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			desc = gal_com_emperors_subject
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_country = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			desc = gal_com_exists_awakened_fallen_empire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			desc = gal_com_ongoing_war_in_heaven
		}
	}

resolution_emperor_repeal_galactic_monitoring_network = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_repeal_galactic_monitoring_network"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			trigger = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" } }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4_half
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		cancel_resolution = "resolution_emperor_galactic_monitoring_network"
		hidden_effect = { pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_imperial_institutions_reset_cooldown }
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_galactic_monitoring_network"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			is_pacifist = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = { is_crisis_faction = yes }
			}
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}

			is_egalitarian = yes

resolution_expel_the_crisis_aspirant = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_declare_crisis"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			trigger = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" } }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" }
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1_half
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = yes
	fire_and_forget = yes

	valid_target = {
		has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
		is_galactic_community_member = yes
	}

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_expel_the_crisis_aspirant_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_subject_of = { who = none }
			country_event = { id = MECR.710 days = 1 } # 防御部队改变
			every_subject = {
				set_subject_of = { who = none }
				country_event = { id = MECR.710 days = 1 } # 防御部队改变
			}
			remove_from_galactic_community = yes
			remove_from_galactic_council = yes
			leave_alliance = { override_requirements = yes }
			clear_imperium_modifiers = yes
			from = {
				pass_targeted_resolution = {
					resolution = resolution_declare_crisis_empire
					target = prev
				}
			}
			pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_imperial_members_reset_cooldown
		}
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			and = {
				has_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular
		modifier = { # Should almost always declare on Crisis countries in end game
			factor = 50
			from = {
				has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = { # More likely to declare on rivals
			factor = 2
			is_rival = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}
		modifier = { # Never on yourself
			factor = 0
			is_same_value = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_me
		}
		modifier = { # More likely to declare on a crisis country that has started cracking stars
			factor = 6
			from = { has_country_flag = cracked_first_star }
			desc = gal_com_target_has_cracked_stars
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			from = {
				has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
			}
			has_intel_level = {
				who = from
				category = government
				level >= 2
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_level_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			from = {
				has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_level_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			from = {
				has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_level_5
		}
	}
}

################################### resolution_category_galactic_lower_house
resolution_form_galactic_lower_house = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_form_galactic_lower_house"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_form_galactic_lower_house_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = form_galactic_lower_house_by_event } }
				set_global_flag = form_galactic_lower_house_by_resolution
				event_target:global_event_country = {
					# 启用时间表局势
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { any_situation = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule } }
						}
						start_situation = {
							type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule
							target = this
						}
					}
					every_situation = {
						limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule }
						export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
							trigger = situation_progress
							variable = situation_progress_var
						}
						multiply_variable = { which = situation_progress_var value = -1 }
						add_situation_progress = situation_progress_var
						add_situation_progress = 65.625
					}
					every_galcom_member = {
						country_event = {
							id = MECR_LH.1010
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = MECR_LH.10
						days = 30
					}
					set_global_flag = lower_house_founded
					set_timed_global_flag = {
						flag = lower_house_form_succeed_timer
						years = 20
					}
					set_saved_date = {
						key = lower_house_form_succeed_date
						days_from_present = 7200
						expires = 7200
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fail_effects = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_form_galactic_lower_house_fail_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_timed_global_flag = {
					flag = lower_house_form_failed_timer
					years = 20
				}
				set_saved_date = {
					key = lower_house_form_failed_date
					days_from_present = 7200
					expires = 7200
				}
				every_galcom_member = {
					country_event = {
						id = MECR_LH.1011
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_wait_for_20_years_to_try_form_lower_house"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = lower_house_repeal_succeed_timer }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_wait_for_20_years_to_try_form_lower_house_again"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = lower_house_form_failed_timer }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "the_lower_house_has_been_founded"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = lower_house_founded }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = lower_house_form_failed
			has_global_flag = lower_house_founded
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_egalitarian = yes
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = value:lower_house_form_effect_relative_power_resolution
			desc = gal_com_relative_power_within_countries
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_galactic_emperor = no
		}
	}
}
resolution_repeal_galactic_lower_house = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_repeal_galactic_lower_house"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_repeal_galactic_lower_house_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				remove_global_flag = lower_house_founded
				set_global_flag = lower_house_form_failed
				set_timed_global_flag = {
					flag = lower_house_repeal_succeed_timer
					years = 20
				}
				set_saved_date = {
					key = lower_house_repeal_succeed_date
					days_from_present = 7200
					expires = 7200
				}
				set_timed_global_flag = {
					flag = instant_stop_lh_session
					years = 6
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = MECR_LH.1020
			}
		}
	}
	fail_effects = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_repeal_galactic_lower_house_fail_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_timed_global_flag = {
					flag = lower_house_repeal_failed_timer
					years = 20
				}
				set_saved_date = {
					key = lower_house_repeal_failed_date
					days_from_present = 7200
					expires = 7200
				}
				every_galcom_member = {
					country_event = {
						id = MECR_LH.1021
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_wait_for_20_years_to_try_repeal_lower_house"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = lower_house_form_succeed_timer }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_wait_for_20_years_to_try_repeal_lower_house_again"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = lower_house_repeal_failed_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = lower_house_founded
		OR = {
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			AND = {
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				OR = {
					has_galactic_emperor = no
					is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_expand_power_of_council"
				}
			}
			is_country_type = imperial_senator
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_hated

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			is_egalitarian = yes
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		modifier = {
			divide = value:lower_house_form_effect_relative_power_resolution
			desc = gal_com_relative_power_within_countries
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_galactic_emperor = no
		}
		modifier = {
			max = 9
			desc = gal_com_resolution
		}
	}
}

resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			galaxy_is_peace = yes
			NOT = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_frozen }
			has_galactic_emperor = no
		}
		modifier = { resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求
		potential = {
			galaxy_is_peace = yes
			NOT = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_frozen }
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			imperial_governance_usage = 100
		}
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_galactic_custodian = no
				has_galactic_emperor = no
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee_effect"
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_galactic_custodian = yes }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee_effect_has_custodian"
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_galactic_emperor = yes }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee_effect_has_emperor"
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee" }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans_or_higher_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans_or_higher_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans
				is_active_resolution = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves
				is_active_resolution = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle
				is_active_resolution = resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate
				is_active_resolution = resolution_greatergood_6
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "galaxy_must_be_peace"
			galaxy_is_peace = yes
		}
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			is_galactic_council_established = yes
			has_galactic_custodian = yes
			has_galactic_emperor = yes
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}

resolution_the_galactic_expo = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_the_galactic_expo"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_the_galactic_expo_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { exists = this }
				country_event = {
					id = MECR_EXPO.1
					days = 1
				}
			}
			else = { #主体国家灭亡的备份方案
				if = {
					limit = { has_galactic_custodian = yes }
					galactic_custodian = {
						country_event = {
							id = MECR_EXPO.1
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_galactic_emperor = yes }
					galactic_emperor = {
						country_event = {
							id = MECR_EXPO.1
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { any_country = { is_permanent_councillor = yes } }
					random_country = {
						limit = { is_permanent_councillor = yes }
						country_event = {
							id = MECR_EXPO.1
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { any_country = { is_part_of_galactic_council = yes } }
					random_country = {
						limit = { is_part_of_galactic_council = yes }
						country_event = {
							id = MECR_EXPO.1
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_country = {
						limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
						country_event = {
							id = MECR_EXPO.1
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = flag_expo_hater }
				remove_country_flag = flag_expo_hater
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_the_galactic_expo" }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_commerce_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_commerce_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_commerce_buzzword_standardization
				is_active_resolution = resolution_commerce_leveraged_privateering
				is_active_resolution = resolution_commerce_underdeveloped_system_utilization
				is_active_resolution = resolution_commerce_holistic_asset_coordination
				is_active_resolution = resolution_commerce_profit_maximization_engines
				is_active_resolution = resolution_commerce_6
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_industry_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_industry_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_regulatory_facilitation
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_collective_waste_management
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_building_a_better_tomorrow
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_environmental_ordinance_waivers
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_project_cornucopia
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_6
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_galacticstudies_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_galacticstudies_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_cooperative_research_channels
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_extradimensional_experimentation
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_6
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "galaxy_must_be_peace"
			galaxy_is_peace = yes
		}
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			is_years_since_community_formation >= 25
			has_global_flag = flag_debug_expo_instant
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_at_war = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_at_war
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			years_of_peace = { value > 9 }
			desc = gal_com_long_peace
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_the_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			desc = galactic_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		cancel_resolution = resolution_the_galactic_expo

			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = flag_expo_preparing
					has_global_flag = flag_expo_ongoing
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_no_more_galactic_expo_effect"
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = flag_expo_hater

			}
		}
	}

			factor = 2

			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2

		}
	}

resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_grading = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_grading"
	resources = { category = resolutions cost = { influence = 10000 } }
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction }
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction_grading"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_science_research }
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_science_research_grading"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_medical_care }
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_medical_care_grading"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy }
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy_grading"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity }
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_grading"
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness } }
				custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_grading_regular"
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_grading_gestalt"
			}
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_grading_additional_a"
			tooltip = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_reward_a days = 3600 } }
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_grading_additional_b"
			tooltip = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_reward_b days = 3600 } }
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_grading_additional_e"
			tooltip = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_denounced days = 3600 } }
			
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_grading_no_five_year_plan"
		}
		no_national_agenda_resolution = yes
	}
	allow = { always = no }
	potential = { any_FYP_ongoing = yes }
	ai_weight = { base = 0 }
}

resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = 50
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_galactic_emperor = no
					has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd
				}
			}
			influence = 25
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd }
			influence = 9925
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction = 1
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_effect_already_active"
		}
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction_effect"

		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction
			set_timed_global_flag = {
				flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd
				years = 5
			}
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_saved_date = {
					key = FYP_timer
					days_from_present = 1800
					expires = 1800
				}
			}
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_formulating
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_formulating_timer
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_frozen
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_kind value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_yes value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_no value = 0 }
				country_event = { id = MECR.501 days = 1 }
			}
			pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_galactic_focus_reset_cooldown
		}
		no_national_agenda_resolution = yes
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "five_year_plan_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "five_year_plan_must_wait_five_years"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee
		galaxy_is_peace = yes
		OR = {
			any_FYP_ongoing = no
			is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction
		}
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		galaxy_is_peace = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				is_galactic_custodian = yes
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_voting_on_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction
				any_country = { is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction }
			}
			desc = gal_com_due_to_fyp_committee
		}
	}
}

		resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy = 1
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_effect_already_active"
		}
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy_effect"
		if = {	# only for harmonious_diplomacy
			limit = { has_galactic_emperor = no }
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy_mission_addition"
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = "galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy_mission_addition_emperor"
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy
			set_timed_global_flag = {
				flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd
				years = 5
			}
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_saved_date = {
					key = FYP_timer
					days_from_present = 1800
					expires = 1800
				}
			}
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_formulating
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_formulating_timer
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_frozen
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_kind value = 4 }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_yes value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_no value = 0 }
				country_event = { id = MECR.501 days = 1 }
			}
			pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_galactic_focus_reset_cooldown
		}
		no_national_agenda_resolution = yes
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "five_year_plan_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "five_year_plan_must_wait_five_years"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee
		galaxy_is_peace = yes
		OR = {
			any_FYP_ongoing = no
			is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy
		}
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		galaxy_is_peace = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				is_galactic_custodian = yes
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_voting_on_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy
				any_country = { is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_harmonious_diplomacy }
			}
			desc = gal_com_due_to_fyp_committee
		}
	}
}
resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = 50
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_galactic_emperor = no
					has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd
				}
			}
			influence = 25
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd }
			influence = 9925
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity = 1
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_effect_already_active"
		}
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity_effect"

		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity
			set_timed_global_flag = {
				flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd
				years = 5
			}
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_saved_date = {
					key = FYP_timer
					days_from_present = 1800
					expires = 1800
				}
			}
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_formulating
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_formulating_timer
			remove_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_frozen
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_kind value = 5 }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_yes value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_no value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = FYP_task_count value = 0 }
				country_event = { id = MECR.503 days = 1 }
			}
			pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_galactic_focus_reset_cooldown
		}
		no_national_agenda_resolution = yes
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "five_year_plan_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_infrastructure_construction }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "five_year_plan_must_wait_five_years"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_cd }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_committee
		galaxy_is_peace = yes
		OR = {
			any_FYP_ongoing = no
			is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity
		}
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		galaxy_is_peace = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_popular
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				is_galactic_custodian = yes
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_voting_on_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity
				any_country = { is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_five_year_plan_shared_prosperity }
			}
			desc = gal_com_due_to_fyp_committee
		}
	}

resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_declare_crisis"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = 50
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" }
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
						NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization" }
					}
				}
			}
			influence = 50
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
				NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization" }
			}
			influence = 9900
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_united_front
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_united_front
			}
		}
		#key = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization_key
		modifier = {
			resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_united_front
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_united_front
			}
		}
		#key = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization_key
		modifier = {
			resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization_united_front = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #无皇帝时的维护费
		potential = { has_galactic_emperor = no }
		#key = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization_key
		modifier = { country_unity_produces_mult = -0.1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求：根据激活的战争命令数量指数增长
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			event_target:global_event_country = { check_variable = { which = constant_1 value >= value:activated_war_orders } }
		}
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 100 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			event_target:global_event_country = { check_variable = { which = constant_2 value = value:activated_war_orders } }
		}
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 200 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			event_target:global_event_country = { check_variable = { which = constant_3 value = value:activated_war_orders } }
		}
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 300 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			event_target:global_event_country = { check_variable = { which = constant_4 value = value:activated_war_orders } }
		}
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 400 }
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
				NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization }
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_effect_will_not_activate"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization_stop"
			cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					#is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
				}
				NOR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
					is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization_effect_switch"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					#is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
				}
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
					is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization_effect_add"
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization_effect"
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization } }
				set_global_flag = galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
				set_timed_global_flag = {
					flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
					years = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
							is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
						}
					}
					#cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
					cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
					cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
					cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
				}
				pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_galactic_focus_reset_cooldown
			}
			else = {
				remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
			}
			set_global_flag = flag_any_war_order_activated
		}
		no_national_agenda_resolution = yes
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "war_order_must_wait_a_year"
			NAND = {
				NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization }
				has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = galactic_community_crisis_fighting
				is_crisis_ongoing = yes
			}
			has_global_flag = flag_imperial_crusade_ongoing
			any_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
		}
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = galactic_community_crisis_fighting
				is_crisis_ongoing = yes
			}
			any_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			resource_income_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value > 1000
			}
			desc = gal_com_economic_situation
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			resource_income_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value > 2000
			}
			desc = gal_com_economic_situation
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
			}
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
			}
			NOR = {
				is_voting_on_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
				any_country = { is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization }
			}
			desc = gal_com_existing_war_order
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
			desc = gal_com_no_cancel_war_order
		}
	}
}

			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
			}
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
			}
			NOR = {
				is_voting_on_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
				any_country = { is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet }
			}
			desc = gal_com_existing_war_order
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
			desc = gal_com_no_cancel_war_order
		}
	}
}
resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_declare_crisis"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = 50
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence" }
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
						NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow" }
					}
				}
			}
			influence = 50
		}
		cost = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
				NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow" }
			}
			influence = 9900
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_extradimensional_invading = no
		}
		#key = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_key
		modifier = {
			resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_extradimensional_invading = yes
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_united_front
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_united_front
			}
		}
		#key = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_key
		modifier = {
			resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_unbidden = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_extradimensional_invading = yes
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_united_front
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_united_front
			}
		}
		#key = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_key
		modifier = {
			resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_unbidden_united_front = 1
		}
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #无皇帝时的维护费
		potential = { has_galactic_emperor = no }
		#key = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_key
		modifier = { country_unity_produces_mult = -0.1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #帝国治理点数需求：根据激活的战争命令数量指数增长
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			event_target:global_event_country = { check_variable = { which = constant_1 value >= value:activated_war_orders } }
		}
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 100 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			event_target:global_event_country = { check_variable = { which = constant_2 value = value:activated_war_orders } }
		}
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 200 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			event_target:global_event_country = { check_variable = { which = constant_3 value = value:activated_war_orders } }
		}
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 300 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			event_target:global_event_country = { check_variable = { which = constant_4 value = value:activated_war_orders } }
		}
		modifier = { imperial_governance_usage = 400 }
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
				NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow }
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_effect_will_not_activate"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow }
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_stop"
			cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
					#is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
				}
				NOR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
					is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_effect_switch"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
					#is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
				}
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
					is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_effect_add"
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow_effect"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_extradimensional_invading = no
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_united_front
					is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_united_front
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = "unlocks_crush_the_crisis_bombardment"
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow } }
				set_global_flag = galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
				set_timed_global_flag = {
					flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
					years = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
							is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
						}
					}
					cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
					cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
					#cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
					cancel_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
				}
				pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_galactic_focus_reset_cooldown
			}
			else = {
				remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
			}
			set_global_flag = flag_any_war_order_activated
		}
		no_national_agenda_resolution = yes
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "war_order_must_wait_a_year"
			NAND = {
				NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow }
				has_global_flag = flag_galactic_focus_war_order_cd
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = galactic_community_crisis_fighting
				is_crisis_ongoing = yes
			}
			has_global_flag = flag_imperial_crusade_ongoing
			any_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
		}
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = galactic_community_crisis_fighting
				is_crisis_ongoing = yes
			}
			any_country = { has_been_declared_crisis = yes }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
			}
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
			}
			NOR = {
				is_voting_on_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
				any_country = { is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow }
			}
			desc = gal_com_existing_war_order
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
			desc = gal_com_no_cancel_war_order
		}
	}
}

		}

				}
			}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					is_crisis_faction = yes
					galaxy_percentage > 0.2
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_military_situation
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_defense_committee
				is_active_resolution = resolution_emperor_imperial_ministry_of_defence
			}
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_industrial_mobilization
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_build_fleet
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_devastating_blow
				is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
			}
			NOR = {
				is_voting_on_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
				any_country = { is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense }
			}
			desc = gal_com_existing_war_order
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_active_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_war_order_planetary_defense
			desc = gal_com_no_cancel_war_order
		}

resolution_galactic_focus_open_imperial_setting_menu = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emperor_imperial_department_of_engineering"
	resources = {
		category = resolutions
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		#custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_focus_open_imperial_setting_menu_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = MECR.999
			}
			pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_galactic_focus_reset_cooldown
		}
		no_national_agenda_resolution = yes
	}

	potential = {
		is_ai = no
		has_galactic_emperor = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
			AND = {
				is_galactic_emperor = no
				galactic_emperor = { is_ai = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		always = no
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = 0
	}
}

################################### resolution_category_confederation_institutions
resolution_custodian_galactic_development_bank = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_custodian_galactic_development_bank"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { is_gal_confed_member = yes }
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_galactic_development_bank = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #upkeep
		potential = { is_gal_confed_member = yes }
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_main_institutions_basic_upkeep_name = 1 }
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_gal_confed_member = no }
			custom_tooltip = "galconfed_resolutions_has_no_effect_for_us"
		}
		else = {
			#custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_development_bank_effect"
			if = {
				limit = { any_federation = { has_federation_perk = trade_galconfed_specialization_bonus_1 } }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_development_bank_upgrade_effects_1"
				if = {
					limit = { any_federation = { has_federation_perk = trade_galconfed_specialization_bonus_2 } }
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_development_bank_upgrade_effects_2"
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_federation = { has_federation_perk = trade_galconfed_specialization_bonus_3 } }
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_development_bank_upgrade_effects_3"
				}
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_galactic_development_bank" }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "galactic_focus_form_the_galactic_market_trigger"
			has_global_flag = galactic_market_founded
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_galactic_standard"
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_gto"
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_commerce_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_commerce_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_buzzword_standardization"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_leveraged_privateering"

	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { is_gestalt = yes }
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_gestalt = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_gal_confed_member = yes
			has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_1
			is_regular_empire = yes
		}
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_1 = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_gal_confed_member = yes
			has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_1
			is_machine_empire = yes
		}
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_1_machine = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_gal_confed_member = yes
			has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_1
			is_hive_empire = yes
		}
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_1_hive = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			is_gal_confed_member = yes
			has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_2
			is_regular_empire = yes
		}
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_2 = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = { #upkeep
		potential = { is_gal_confed_member = yes }
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_sub_institutions_basic_upkeep_name = 1 }
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "[Get_resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_level]"
		if = {
			limit = { is_gal_confed_member = no }
			custom_tooltip = "galconfed_resolutions_has_no_effect_for_us"
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_gestalt = no }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_1 } }
					custom_tooltip = "gestalt_empires_will_get"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers_gestalt"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_sub_institutions_basic_upkeep"
					custom_tooltip = "as_regular_empire_we_will_get"
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_2 } }
					custom_tooltip = "gestalt_empires_will_get"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers_gestalt"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers_1_gestalt"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_sub_institutions_basic_upkeep"
					custom_tooltip = "as_regular_empire_we_will_get"
				}
				else = {
					custom_tooltip = "gestalt_empires_will_get"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers_gestalt"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers_1_gestalt"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_effect_2_gestalt"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_sub_institutions_basic_upkeep"
					custom_tooltip = "as_regular_empire_we_will_get"
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_1 } }
					custom_tooltip = "regular_empires_will_get"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_sub_institutions_basic_upkeep"
					custom_tooltip = "as_gestalt_empire_we_will_get"
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_upgrade_2 } }
					custom_tooltip = "regular_empires_will_get"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers_1"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_sub_institutions_basic_upkeep"
					custom_tooltip = "as_gestalt_empire_we_will_get"
				}
				else = {
					custom_tooltip = "regular_empires_will_get"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers_1"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_modifiers_2"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_sub_institutions_basic_upkeep"
					custom_tooltip = "as_gestalt_empire_we_will_get"
					custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_confed_galpol_effect_2_gestalt"
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_custodian_galpol
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = yes
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_establish_the_galactic_confederation
	}

		has_nemesis = yes
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {

		}

		modifier = {

			desc = gov_criminal_syndicate

			}
		}
	}

	potential = {

resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit = {  
	icon = "GFX_resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { is_gal_confed_member = yes }
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit = 1 }
	}
	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = { is_gal_confed_member = yes has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_upgrade_1 }
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_upgrade_1 = 1 }
	}
	#triggered_modifier = {
	#	potential = { is_gal_confed_member = yes has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_upgrade_2 }
	#	modifier = { resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_upgrade_2 = 1 }
	#}
	triggered_modifier = { #upkeep
		potential = { is_gal_confed_member = yes }
		modifier = { resolution_custodian_sub_institutions_basic_upkeep_name = 1 }
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "[Get_resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_level]"
		if = {
			limit = { is_gal_confed_member = no }
			custom_tooltip = "galconfed_resolutions_has_no_effect_for_us"
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_effect"
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit } }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_effect_tech"
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_upgrade_2 }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_effect_2"
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_tech_0 } }
					set_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit_tech_0
					every_galcom_member = {
						limit = { is_gal_confed_member = yes }
						add_research_option = tech_mining_2
						add_research_option = tech_mining_3
						add_research_option = tech_mineral_purification_1
						add_research_option = tech_mineral_purification_2
			
						add_research_option = tech_mine_volatile_motes
						add_research_option = tech_mine_exotic_gases
						add_research_option = tech_mine_rare_crystals
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_exploit" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_galactic_standard"
		OR = {
			has_active_tradition = tr_prosperity_finish
			any_council_member = { has_active_tradition = tr_prosperity_finish }
		}
		#is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_assist_the_developing_countries"
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_industry_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_industry_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_regulatory_facilitation
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_collective_waste_management
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_building_a_better_tomorrow
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_environmental_ordinance_waivers
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_project_cornucopia
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_6
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		has_federation = yes
		federation = { has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive }
		OR = {
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			is_federation_leader = yes
		}
	}

	active = {
		OR = {
			has_galactic_custodian = yes
			any_federation = { has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				resource_income_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value < 300
				}
				resource_income_compare = {
					resource = minerals
					value < 500
				}
				resource_income_compare = {
					resource = food
					value < 200
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_economic_situation
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				resource_income_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value < 0
				}
				resource_income_compare = {
					resource = minerals
					value < 0
				}
				resource_income_compare = {
					resource = food
					value < 0
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_economic_situation
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					is_crisis_faction = yes
					has_country_flag = declared_crisis
					has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = galactic_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}
