			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering" }
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_galactic_standard"
		has_technology = tech_assembly_pattern
		has_technology = tech_construction_templates
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = "must_have_resolution_industry_yes"
			fail_text = "must_have_resolution_industry_no"
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_regulatory_facilitation
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_collective_waste_management
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_building_a_better_tomorrow
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_environmental_ordinance_waivers
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_project_cornucopia
				is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_6
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		has_federation = yes
		federation = { has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive }
		OR = {
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			is_federation_leader = yes
		}
	}

	active = {
		OR = {
			has_galactic_custodian = yes
			any_federation = { has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			count_owned_planet = {
				count >= 3
				limit = {
					has_upgraded_capital = no
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_has_planets_for_construction
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			resource_income_compare = {
				resource = minerals
				value < 300
			}
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = minerals
				value < 7200
			}
			desc = gal_com_economic_situation
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = galactic_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}
}
resolution_custodian_upgrade_galactic_department_of_engineering = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_custodian_upgrade_galactic_department_of_engineering"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_gal_confed_member = no }
			custom_tooltip = "galconfed_resolutions_has_no_effect_for_us"
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_upgrade_1 } }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_effect_1"
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_effect_1_tech"
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_modifier_1"
				hidden_effect = {
					every_galcom_member = {
						limit = { is_gal_confed_member = yes }
						add_research_option = tech_mega_engineering
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_upgrade_2 } }
				custom_tooltip = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_modifier_2"
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_upgrade_1 } }
				set_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_upgrade_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_upgrade_2 } }
				set_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_upgrade_2
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		has_technology = tech_mega_engineering
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "requires_galconfed_higher_centralization_no"
			any_federation = {
				has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive
				check_variable = { which = centralization_institution_upgrades_cap value > value:confed_institutions_levels }
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering
		NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering_upgrade_2 }
		has_nemesis = yes
		has_federation = yes
		OR = {
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			is_federation_leader = yes
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			resource_income_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value < 300
			}
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value < 7200
			}
			desc = gal_com_economic_situation
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			resource_income_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value > 1000
			}
			has_technology = tech_mega_engineering
			desc = gal_com_ready_for_mega_engineering
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					is_crisis_faction = yes
					has_country_flag = declared_crisis
					has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = galactic_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}
}

		}

	potential = {
		has_nemesis = yes
		has_federation = yes
		federation = { has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive }
		OR = {
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			is_federation_leader = yes
		}
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_custodian_galactic_department_of_engineering"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			resource_income_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value < 0
			}
			desc = gal_com_economic_situation
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					is_crisis_faction = yes
					has_country_flag = declared_crisis
					has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_someone_is_revealed_crisis
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			desc = galactic_custodian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			is_galactic_custodian = no
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
	}

################################### resolution_category_confederation_members
resolution_galactic_confederation_kick_member = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_confederation_kick_member"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = yes
	fire_and_forget = yes

	valid_target = {
		NOT = { is_same_value = from }
		is_galactic_custodian = no
		has_federation = yes
		is_federation_leader = no
		federation = { has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive }
	}

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "resolution_galactic_confederation_kick_member_effect"
		hidden_effect = {
			leave_alliance = { override_requirements = yes }
			remove_from_galactic_community = yes
			remove_from_galactic_council = yes
			pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_category_confederation_members_reset_cooldown
		}
		no_national_agenda_resolution = yes
	}

	potential = {
		has_federation = yes
		is_federation_leader = no
		federation = {
			has_federation_perk = galactic_confederation_passive
			has_federation_law = kick_members_senate_confederation
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		modifier = { # Should almost always declare on Crisis countries in end game
			factor = 50
			from = {
				has_country_flag = crisis_sphere_revealed
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_sphere_revealed
		}
		modifier = { # More likely to declare on rivals
			factor = 5
			is_rival = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}
		modifier = { # Never on yourself
			factor = 0
			is_same_value = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_me
		}
		modifier = { # More likely to declare on a crisis country that has started cracking stars
			factor = 6
			from = { has_country_flag = cracked_first_star }
			desc = gal_com_target_has_cracked_stars
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			from = {
				has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
			}
			has_intel_level = {
				who = from
				category = government
				level >= 2
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_level_3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			from = {
				has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_level_4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			from = {
				has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
			}
			desc = gal_com_crisis_level_5
		}
	}
}
resolution_category_confederation_members_reset_cooldown = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_confederation_members"
	resources = { category = resolutions }
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes
	effect = { no_national_agenda_resolution = yes }
	allow = { always = no }
	potential = { always = no }
	ai_weight = { base = 0 }
}
